<Text>I heard that USD is an excellent private university. They have highly accredited teaching, law, technology, language, environmental and psychology schools, as well as a number of others. I also heard that their physical education school is quite good.
USD is one of our nation's top rated colleges in regards to higher education and just to get admitted, you must score fairly high on the SAT ( Taking the ACT can always helps too ) and presenting the admissions evaluation committee with a high school GPA that shows that you were in the top percentile of your graduating class is very beneficial; it also helps to have done some volunteer work and to have been on at least one or two high school committees. All of these combined together should help you gain admission to USD.
This college is quite competitive-as are most of our best colleges nowadays. Most of USD's professors are seasoned-the best in our country-and very demanding; graduating in four years means a lot of hard work and can be a wearisome task and often taking a couple of summer session classes or a class or two during Christmas break can help one graduate within this time scale.
They do offer scholarships however, these are difficult to get and student loans ( Federal Educational Grants can easily surpass fifty-thousand dollars a year!
USD's tuition is at the high end of the scale, especially if you live off of campus ( The City of San Diego is amongst the ten highest priced "cost of living" metropolitan areas in the USA ). There are hundreds of nice condominiums, townhouses and apartments within the surrounding area however, the rental rates for a one to four bedroom unit start at about $900 to $1200 per room ( living together ) per month or about $2200 for a two bedroom townhouse/apartment, to $3500+ for a three to four bedroom ; I'm just giving you a general idea...it's a might expensive to live anywhere in San Diego.
USD has many of the most beautifully designed buildings in San Diego; architectural masterpieces. Tourists who come to visit San Diego often include this private university in their sightseeing itinerary, as the photographic opportunities around this campus are simply marvelous; especially on a clear winter day from about early afternoon to sunset.
They have a small visitors center, as you drive through their main entrance center and if you get lost, you should stop and ask a couple of students and they may be able to help you?
There's a lot to see, including San Diego's famed Tecalote State Park, which lies just below the north side of this university.< /Text><Pics>None</Pics><date>1541396299837</date><Response>None< /Response></record>

< text>
As a university USD fails in a lot of the ways other American school's do-- in the cost. It's a very expensive place to learn. There are a lot of amazing people at the University who seem to really care about their jobs, the students, and their community.
The food is incredibly expensive on campus, and it's private with no outside businesses providing food, which they spin as a good thing, but regardless it isolates lower income students who can't afford to eat on campus.
The trams don't run on a reliable time schedule and parking is difficult. It's also difficult to walk from the parking structures to the main campus because it's very hilly.
If you're looking for a place with great staff, USD is up there. Though you could get an equal education for much less in price I'm sure.</text>

< review>
A very beautiful school. Well kept and great campus. Unfortunately, USD is not all hyped up like people think. It is difficult to get the classes that you want (also due to the few amount of courses available). The tuition is very expensive and it seems to just be going to the aesthetic of the campus. You have to do everything their way or you get nothing.
Thought that this school would set me and my mates up for job careers and help us find jobs, but no such luck thus far.
After graduating, all they keep asking for is money and not once do they ever ask to help you look for a job.
Make sure you dont just get distracted by the look of the school. Yes, it is a beautiful campus with an ocean view, but there is more to USD that meets the eye. Do your research before coming here!< /review>

On Thursday, the first full day in office for San Diego‚Äôs new Catholic bishop, the Catholic University of San Diego (USD) hosted a ‚Äúdrag show‚Äù that the Vatican last year described as ‚Äúscandalous.‚Äù Attorney Charles LiMandri, who founded Alumni for a Catholic USD and helped file a petition to the Vatican against the University‚Äôs annual cross-dressing event, spoke with The Cardinal Newman Society to discuss why USD is continuing to ignore the Vatican and even the recent words of Pope Francis.Last year, the Vatican‚Äôs Congregation for Catholic Education responded to the petition submitted by LiMandri and Thomas McKenna, founder and president of Catholic Action for Faith and Family. The Congregation‚Äôs letter deemed the drag show a ‚Äúscandal‚Äù and declared its intentions ‚Äúto act through administrative channels to the competent ecclesiastical authority in San Diego.‚Äù Whether under the guise of diversity or not, there is no excuse for a Catholic college to ignore the Vatican, LiMandri explained:

People that supposedly share our beliefs are grossly misrepresenting them and are getting a free pass. Even after they‚Äôve been told by the highest authority [in the Catholic Church] that what they‚Äôre doing is scandalous‚Äîwhich in Church parlance has specific meaning‚Äîthat you are leading people away from the faith, it is causing a potential loss of faith. The people who are in a position to represent the faith are giving a bad example. In this case it is not just a bad example, but it is a fraudulent message. They‚Äôre misrepresenting what the Church teaches, and you can‚Äôt get away with that under the guise of diversity.

Pope Francis addressed gender theory in his Wednesday audience this week, the day before the USD drag show:

As we all know, sexual difference is present in so many forms of life, in the long scale of the living. However, only in man and in woman does it bear in itself the image and likeness of God‚Ä¶ Man and woman are [the] image and likeness of God!

‚Ä¶ Modern and contemporary culture has opened new areas, new freedoms and new depths for the enrichment of the understanding of this difference. However, it has also introduced many doubts and much skepticism. For instance, I wonder, for example, if the so-called gender theory is not also an expression of a frustration and of a resignation, which aims to cancel the sexual difference because it no longer knows how to address it. Yes, we risk taking a step backward. The removal of the difference, in fact, is the problem, not the solution. To resolve their problems of relation, man and woman must instead talk more to one another, listen more to one another, know one another more, love one another more.

LiMandri hopes that USD might be a better example to these colleges.

‚ÄúMy goal and desire in a very personal way is to see USD come back into the fold like the prodigal son,‚Äù he said. ‚ÄúI love USD. I want to see USD be the best that she can be, that‚Äôs what is motivating me. I want to see USD get back on track, in line with the vision of its founders and what they profess in their mission statement.‚Äù

‚ÄúThese are good students who are being deprived of a good Catholic education,‚Äù he added. ‚ÄúWhen we get the word out and Catholics rally, good things can and do result.‚Äù

Until the University once again embraces the teachings of Christ, this gets one star.<//Text>

< text>
Visiting high school students need to be aware that USD will add you to their system(s).  My son visited USD in the Fall of 2012 and he just rec'd a "Final Notice of Non-payment".  He had 1 week to pay/resolve or it was going to be turned over to a collection agency.  He received no other notices.
Turns out he has a Student ID even though he never applied to USD.  All he did was visit.  There was a keystroke error in Housing and he ended up with a $5,000+ bill.  We are working to clear up the confusion but visiting high school students need to read all forms to understand what USD will do with your personal information.
I have requested a copy of their Privacy Policy - better read it very closely!</text>

<Date>1565061349900< /Date><Rate>3</Rate>< Text>
Saw the strip mall from the train station and went looking for lunch. A friendly employee asked if she could help me. I asked what brand of  pastrami they served. She said they get it from a large supplier that delivers. Couldn't chance the unknown pastrami. But, they didn‚Äôt serve corn beef, so I couldn‚Äôt make the classic deli meat combo anyway.

Ordered a hot sandwich with ham, dry salami, and cheddar on sourdough combo (2 meat + cheese selection, chips & drink total under $9.00). Received a sandwich with warmed bread (not toasted) and cool meat and cheese. The meat portion was on the small side, basically one slice of each, plus a pre-cut slice of cheese. The bread was more white than sourdough, but it was very fresh.

The combo comes with a choice from a large selection chips, and the soda selection is Coke brands.

Overall, it was above the usual convenience store fare. A good variety of choice of sandwiches and non-sandwich selections will provide a decent meal for anyone. The convenience store inventory provides make-your-own meal possibilities, if that suits you better.<//Text>

I was very skeptical on sending in my drone after it crashed and the gimbal was removed from the original position. I bought the DJI Care Refresh package as well when I bought the DJI Mavic Air 2, so I felt a little better about sending it in.

I was also on a quick timeline because I was moving out of town and needed to to have the drone back in a matter of two weeks.

With all that being said, once you get your case number, you can check the status of your drone and the repair process. Within the first day, I received a notice that they were assessing the damages.

The next day, I received a report of the damages.

The next day, I received an invoice to pay for my replacement drone ($69) for the first replacement with the DJI Care Package.

Then, received my drone the following Monday. So it was a one week turn around. I might've even received that Friday. I can't remember.

However, I am writing a very different review and I was very happy with how they followed through with the DJI care refresh package and also the turn around time. So thank you DJI!<//Text>

< Text>
Oh boy, 8 minutes go by really fast.
I drive an Expedition, so being that it's a big vehicle washing it does take time. I opted for the five dollar option, which gave me 8 minutes in which to wet/soap, brush and rinse the car, but that wasn't enough time to get it done. I added to more minutes by inserting a dollar, and that seemed to do the trick.
The equipment worked well. I really like the fact that you can now pay with bills and credit card. The soap was plentiful and the water pressure was enough to remove all the grime from the crevices.
Great price. Great experience.< /Text>

< review>
Good mechanics are hard to come by and trust worthy ones are rare.  Despite all the negative comments I took a chance and stopped by Deep's to have my wife's hub bearings replaced on her 2012 Honda Civic due to the shops proximity to my home.  On June 26 I stopped by and spoke with Bee to get a quote.  Despite exceeding his closing hour of 5:30PM, Bee stayed open and helped me obtain a quote.  He even had one of his repair techs take my wife's vehicle out for a test drive.  On June  27 my wife dropped off her car at 8AM and I received a call from Deep's at noon stating that my wife's car was ready for pickup.  My experience with Deep's Auto Repair has been nothing but positive.  From their willingness to staying the extra hour to help, to their fast turn around, I will surely be using their services in the future.  Also, as a side note, their charge for the repair was lower then other shops that I had called.  Thank you  Deep's.< /review>

<gmapID>0x80c29a53e6cc26e1:0x9050744ee1c73a4b</gmapID>< text>
I'm so glad such an amazing venue opened up here in the Valley.  My wife and I have gone to handful of shows here every year and have been disappointed.  First, the venue is a work of art.  It's beautiful on the outside and gorgeous on the inside.  The acoustics inside the theatre are fantastic.  There's not a bad seat in the house.  We saw La Santa Cecilia there last year and La Marisoul went acoustic for a song and could hear her clearly in the back of the theatre.  Second, they have amazing shows!  From the aforementioned La Santa Cecilia/La Marisoul to the Aspen Santa Fe ballet to David Sedaris to W Kamau Bell, they really book a variety of fantastic shows and artists. < Text>
I have been lucky enough to attend a few shows and presentations at the Valley Performing Arts Center (VPAC). It is a state of the art and elegant venue on the CSUN campus. It is not a large but a decent sized venue with each seat having a great view of the stage.

Each show is professionally staffed with individuals that assists you with finding your seats and to answer any questions you may have. They are also there to enforce the no flash photography policy during shows.

For those of you who live quite a ways from the venue, you will have the option at staying at the Hyatt hotel that will be built right across the street from the VPAC in the near future. The hotel will open in mid 2019.<//Text>

And if you have any physical limitations,  your handicap placard is basically useless unless you decide to show up 3 hours in advance.  I attended an event at the Valley PAC on 9/30 and one at the Hollywood Bowl on 10/1 and the difference in the parking between the two venues is stark - at VPAC, we had to walk at least 3/4 of a mile to & from the car (since i was on crutches,  i only had to do this once, but my partner had to park the car, walk the length of the parking lot to get to the kiosk to pay for parking, walk BACK to the car to put the parking receipt on the dashboard, then walk it AGAIN to get to the theater,  then again after the show - outrageous), whereas at the Bowl (where there is generous handicap parking or the option to take shuttle buses directly  to the main entrance from anywhere in the greater LA area) we were in our car and on our way home in minutes.  And the event at VPAC maybe had 1,000 people in attendance, whereas the Bowl was sold out and 18,000 people were navigating the venue.  Not to mention the VPAC lot was virtually pitch black at night, making a terrible situation even worse due to the dangerous conditions. <name>Jessica Mayes< /name><Date>1562622306419< /Date><rate>1</rate>< Review>
Honestly the worst taco bell I've been to. Terrible quality control. We go in every once in a while if I dont feel like cooking dinner and there is ALWAYS something wrong with the order. The food is always lopside (meaning the ingredients are not throughout the item, such as a crunchwrap having all the meat at the bottom, lettuce tomatoes in the middle and sour cream/cheese on top?) Its to the point I dont even order a crunchwrap anymore, that's not the only item this happens with but just an example. I've gotten a simple soft taco and gotten home to realize there was no meat, only cheese and lettuce... the one thing I can say is that the workers work FAST. But once you get your meal it's literally slopped together, and all thrown into ONE bag...so everything is squashed anyway. You dont put a grilled stuff burrito on top of crunchy tacos and a gordita... it makes at least half the meal inedible. We just wont come anymore, it's not worth being disappointed and having to find something else to eat anyway. Save your time and money.</Review>

This place is not only slow, it's disgusting.

On a recent Friday night a friend wanted some quick Taco Bell. As we pulled up, the drive thru was packed. So we went inside

The reason the drive through was so busy?

The only reason I could figure is, the place smelled like a bathroom! And in not a nice way. That smell when it seems like the sewer is backing up and coming out thru the toilet.

My friend commented about it to the counter person. She just looked at us with a blank stare.

How can a food prep place smell like a backed up sewer? I've been in porta pottys that smell better.

Perhaps the selection of fast food is slim to none in rosamond. But no way would I ever go back. Not even in the drive thru. Food served in a place that filthy is disgusting.

Pass.</review>
